//总秒数
var maxtime ='3600';
	function CountDown(){  
		 if(maxtime>=0){
			 maxtime--; 
		 	var  minutes = Math.floor(maxtime/60);
			var  seconds = Math.floor(Number(maxtime)%60);  
			if(minutes<10 ){
				minutes="0"+minutes;
			}
			if(seconds<10 ){
				seconds="0"+seconds;
			}
			var msg =minutes+":"+seconds;
			if(minutes>=0 && seconds>=0){
				$("#countdown").html("剩余时间："+msg); 
			}
		 	
		 	//大于5分钟给出提示
		 	//if(maxtime>=300){
		 		//if(maxtime == 5*60){
			  		//alertShow("抓紧时间喔，还有5分钟！"); 
			 	//}
		 	//}
		 	if(maxtime<0){  
			 		clearInterval(timer);  
			 		alertSureClose("时间到，本次自测将自动提交！",function(){
						saveStuAnswer('submitAnswer',true);
					});
			}
			   
		}
	}

		var timer = setInterval("CountDown()",1000);

	
//总共几道题
var questionNum=0;
function saveStuAnswer(saveStyle,timingOver){
		
	questionNum = $("ul.testQuestions li").size();
	var token = $("input:hidden[name='token']").val();	
	//清除form中所有的答案
	$("#submitStuAnswer").empty();
	$("#submitStuAnswer").append("<input type=\"hidden\" name=\"struts.token.name\" value=\"token\" />");
	$("#submitStuAnswer").append("<input type=\"hidden\" name=\"token\" value=\"" + token +"\" />");
	//判断题
	var trueOrFalseItems ="";
	//单选题
	var singleTopicSelection="";
	//多选题
	var checkedBox="";
	//不定项选择
	var uncertainSelection="";
		
	$("ul.testQuestions li").each(function(){
			
		//找到每道试题		
			var questionType = $(this).find(".classtype").val(); 
			
			if(questionType == 1){ //单选
				
					var questionID = $(this).find(".hiddenScoreAndId").val();
					var checkedVal=$(this).find(":radio:checked").val();
					var questionIDAndVal="";
					if(checkedVal==undefined){
						questionIDAndVal=questionID+":,";
					}else{
						if(questionNum>0){
							questionNum--;
						}
						questionIDAndVal=questionID+":"+checkedVal+",";
					}
					singleTopicSelection+=questionIDAndVal;
			}else if(questionType == 2){ //多选
				
					var questionID = $(this).find(".hiddenScoreAndId").val();
					var checkedVal="";
					$(this).find(":checkbox:checked").each(function(){
						checkedVal+=$(this).val()+"-";
					});
					if($(this).find(":checkbox:checked").size()>0){
						if(questionNum>0){
							questionNum--;
						}
					}
					var questionIDAndVal = questionID+":"+checkedVal+",";
					checkedBox+=questionIDAndVal;
			}else if(questionType == 3){ //填空
				
					var questionID = $(this).find(".hiddenScoreAndId").val();
					var checkedVal="";
					var biao=-1;
					$(this).find("input.Fill_Input").each(function(){
						if($(this).val().trim()==null || $(this).val().trim()==""){
							noAnswer=1;
							checkedVal+="<span class=\"stuFillOutAnswer\"></span>";
						}else{
							biao=0;
							var stuAnswerOver=html_encode($(this).val());
							checkedVal+="<span class=\"stuFillOutAnswer\">"+stuAnswerOver+"</span>";
						}
					});
					if(biao==0){
						if(questionNum>0){
								questionNum--;
						}
					}
					var questionIDAndVal = questionID+":"+checkedVal;
					//分开为了避免特殊字符再给我转成HTML标签
					var ele = $("<input type='hidden' name='fillOut'/>");
					ele.val(questionIDAndVal);
					$("#submitStuAnswer").append(ele);
			}else if(questionType == 5){ //判断
				
					var questionID = $(this).find(".hiddenScoreAndId").val();
					var checkedVal=$(this).find(":radio:checked").val();
					var questionIDAndVal ="";
					if(checkedVal==undefined){
						questionIDAndVal=questionID+":,";
					}else{
						if(questionNum>0){
							questionNum--;
						}
						questionIDAndVal=questionID+":"+checkedVal+",";
					}
					trueOrFalseItems += questionIDAndVal;	
			}else if(questionType == 6){ //不定项选择
				
					var questionID = $(this).find(".hiddenScoreAndId").val();
					var checkedVal="";
					$(this).find(":checkbox:checked").each(function(){
						checkedVal+=$(this).val()+"-";
					});
					if($(this).find(":checkbox:checked").size()>0){
						if(questionNum>0){
							questionNum--;
						}
					}
					var questionIDAndVal = questionID+":"+checkedVal+",";
					uncertainSelection+=questionIDAndVal;
			}
		});

		$("#submitStuAnswer").append("<input type='hidden' name='singleTopicSelection' value='"+singleTopicSelection+"'/>");
		$("#submitStuAnswer").append("<input type='hidden' name='checkedBox' value='"+checkedBox+"'/>");
		$("#submitStuAnswer").append("<input type='hidden' name='trueOrFalseItems' value='"+trueOrFalseItems+"'/>");
		$("#submitStuAnswer").append("<input type='hidden' name='uncertainSelection' value='"+uncertainSelection+"'/>");
		
		
		$("#submitStuAnswer").append("<input type='hidden' name='stuSelfExamInfoId' value='5000711363'/>");
		
		$("#submitStuAnswer").append("<input type='hidden' name='testPaperTacticsId' value='5000000177'/>");
		
		//提交或暂存
		if(saveStyle=="submitAnswer"){
			$("#submitStuAnswer").append("<input type='hidden' name='mode' value='1'/>");
			//定时到期自动提交
			if(timingOver){
				$("#submitButtonDiv").hide();
				$("#submitStuAnswer").attr("action","saveStuAnswer.action");
				$("#submitStuAnswer").submit();
				return;
			}
			//提示是否答完全部题
			if(questionNum==0){
				confirmShow("您已答完全部试题，确认提交吗？",function() {
					$("#submitButtonDiv").hide();
					$("#submitStuAnswer").attr("action","saveStuAnswer.action");
					$("#submitStuAnswer").submit();
				});		
			}else{
				confirmShow("您还有"+questionNum+"道题未作答，确认提交吗？",function() {
					$("#submitButtonDiv").hide();
					$("#submitStuAnswer").attr("action","saveStuAnswer.action");
					$("#submitStuAnswer").submit();
				});	
			}
		
		}else{
			$("#submitStuAnswer").append("<input type='hidden' name='mode' value='0'/>");
			confirmShow("确认暂存吗？",function() {
				$.post("saveStuAnswer2.action",$("#submitStuAnswer").serialize(),function(data){
					alertShow(data);
				});
			});
		}
}
//显示单项选择题的答案
function singleSelectionShowAnswer(thisObject){
			//获取radio后的字母,
			var radioNextVal=$(thisObject).next().html();
			
			//去掉'.';
			radioNextVal=radioNextVal.split("."); 
			
			//在横杠上显示
			$(thisObject).parent().parent().parent().parent().siblings(".actvie_type").val(radioNextVal[0].trim());
			
}
//显示多选的答案
function checkboxShowAnswer(thisObject,isCheckBoxOrUncertainSelection){
	
			//获取同辈的checkBox元素
			var siblingObject=$(thisObject).parent().parent().parent().parent().find("input[name^='"+isCheckBoxOrUncertainSelection+"']");
			 var checkboxValue="";
			for(var i=0;i<siblingObject.size();i++){
				if(siblingObject[i].checked){
					//获取radio后的字母,
					var checkboxNextVal=$(siblingObject[i]).next().html();
					//alert(checkboxNextVal);
					//去掉'.';
					checkboxNextVal=checkboxNextVal.split("."); 
					checkboxValue+=checkboxNextVal[0].trim();
				}
				
			}
			//横杠上的值
			$(thisObject).parent().parent().parent().parent().siblings(".actvie_type").val(checkboxValue);
}

$(function(){
	
		$(".actvie_type").each(function(){
			$(this).attr("readonly",true);
		});
			//暂存或提交过来的时候，显示学生答案或正确答案
			$("ul.testQuestions").each(function(){
				//找每个小题
				$(this).find("li").each(function(){
						//题型
						var questionType = $(this).find(".classtype").val(); 
						
						if(questionType == 1){ //单选题
							
								//正确答案的Id
								var okAnswer =$(this).find("input.singleAnswer").val();
									
								//学生答案
								var stuAnswer=$(this).find("input.stuSingleAnswer").val();
								if(stuAnswer!=null &&  stuAnswer!=0 ){
										//学生答案所对应的字母
										var  stuAnswerNextVal = $("#single"+stuAnswer).next().html();
										stuAnswerNextVal=stuAnswerNextVal.split(".");
										
										//把学生的答案赋给横杠
										$(this).find("input.actvie_type").val(stuAnswerNextVal[0].trim());
								}
								
								
						}else if(questionType == 2){ //多选题
							
								 //正确答案所对应的字母，ABCD
								 var manyOkAnswerVals= "";
								 var okAnswer =$(this).find("input.manyAnswer");
								 //去拼正确答案对应的字母
								 okAnswer.each(function(){
									  var  okAnswerVal = $(this).val();
									  var  okAnswerNextVal = $("#manySelect"+okAnswerVal).next().html();
									  okAnswerNextVal=okAnswerNextVal.split(".");
									  manyOkAnswerVals+=okAnswerNextVal[0].trim();
									 
								 });
							 	
								//学生答案
								var stuAnswer =$(this).find("input.stuManySelectAnswer").val();
								if(stuAnswer!=null && stuAnswer!=0){
									 var stuAnswerArray = stuAnswer.split(",");
									 stuAnswer="";
									 for(var i=0 ;i<stuAnswerArray.length;i++){	 
										  $("#manySelect"+stuAnswerArray[i]).attr("checked",true);
										 var  okAnswerNextVal = $("#manySelect"+stuAnswerArray[i]).next().html();
										  okAnswerNextVal=okAnswerNextVal.split(".");
										  stuAnswer+=okAnswerNextVal[0].trim();
									 }
								}	
								//把学生的答案赋给横杠
								$(this).find("input.actvie_type").val(stuAnswer);
							 	
								
						}else if(questionType == 3){ //填空题
							
							    //每个横杠对象
								var  fillInputObject=$(this).find("input.Fill_Input");
								 //学生每个填空的对象集合
								var stuAnswerObject=$(this).find("input.stufillOutAnswer");
								if(stuAnswerObject!=null && stuAnswerObject.length>0){
									//循环该题下学生的每填空的答案
									for(var i=0;i<stuAnswerObject.length;i++){
										//学生每空答案
										 var stuAnswer =$(stuAnswerObject.get(i)).val();
										var istrue=false; 
										//一个空的正确答案对象
										var oneFillObject=$(this).find(".eachFillAnswer"+(i+1));
										for(var w=0;w<oneFillObject.length;w++){
											if(stuAnswer==$(oneFillObject[w]).val().trim()){
												istrue = true;
												break;
											}
										}
										
										//为每个空判上对错号
										if(istrue==true){
											 $(fillInputObject.get(i)).after("<font>&nbsp;</font><img class='fault' alt='correct' src='images/right_read.jpg'>");
										}else{
											 $(fillInputObject.get(i)).after("<font>&nbsp;</font><img class='fault' alt='correct' src='images/fault.jpg'>");
										}
										 if(stuAnswer!=null){
											 //放到横杠上
											 $(fillInputObject.get(i)).val(stuAnswer);
											 //横杠不可用
											  
										 }
									}
								}
						
						}else if(questionType == 5){ //判断题
							
								
		
						}else if(questionType == 6){ //不定项选择
								
								//显示正确答案
							 	
								//处理每题得分的位置
								 var isCertain=$(this).find(".correct").html();
								if(isCertain==null && ""==0){
									$(this).append("<span class='quest_content' id='haha'><font style='width: 42px;'></font></span>");
									$(this).find("#haha").append($(this).find(".noManyScore"));
								}else{
									$(this).find(".correct").parent().append($(this).find(".noManyScore"));
								}
							 	//学生答案
								var stuAnswer =$(this).find("input.stuManySelectAnswer").val();
								if(stuAnswer!=null && stuAnswer!=0){
									 var stuAnswerArray = stuAnswer.split(",");
									 stuAnswer="";
									 for(var i=0 ;i<stuAnswerArray.length;i++){ 
										 $("#manySelect"+stuAnswerArray[i]).attr("checked",true);
										 var  okAnswerNextVal = $("#manySelect"+stuAnswerArray[i]).next().html();
										  okAnswerNextVal=okAnswerNextVal.split(".");
										  stuAnswer+=okAnswerNextVal[0].trim();
									 }
								}	
								 //把学生的答案赋给横杠
								$(this).find("input.actvie_type").val(stuAnswer);
							 	//隐藏多选框
							 	
							
						}
				});
			});
	
})

<script type="text/javascript">
function isEqualsCourseAjax(curr,courseId){
	$(curr).bind("click" , function(){
		$.ajax( {
			url : "isCurrentCourseInfoIdAjax.action?d=" + new Date().getTime(),
			type : "post",
			async : false,
			data : {"courseInfoId" : courseId},
			dataType : "json",
			success : function(data) {
				if(data.isEquals == 1){
					top.location.href = "exit.action?message=clearCourse";

				}
				else if (data.isEquals == 2) {
					top.location.href = "exit.action?message=equalsCourse";
				}
			}
		});
	});
}

$(document).ready(function(){
	var isEqualsCourse = function(){
		var courseId = "5000000407";
		if("" == courseId){
			return;
		}else{
			isEqualsCourseAjax(this,courseId);
			$("iframe").each(function(){
				$(this).bind("load",function(){
					var current = this.contentWindow.document.body;
					isEqualsCourseAjax(current,courseId);
				})
				
			});
		}
	};
	isEqualsCourse();
});
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">

function openWin(targetName){
	var winHeight = $(top.document).height();
	var boxWidth = $(targetName).width();
	var boxHeight = $(targetName).height();
	
	var coverHeight = $(top.document).height();
	function yAxis(){
		if($("div.winCover").length == 0){
			$('body').append("<div class='winCover'></div>");
			$(targetName).css({'margin-left':-(boxWidth/2)});
			$(targetName).css("top",20+$(document).scrollTop()).show();
			$('.winCover').css('height',coverHeight);
		}
	}
	yAxis();
}

//截取字符串
function cutstr(str,len){
	if( undefined == str){
		return false;
	}
	var str_length = 0;
	var str_len = 0;
	str_cut = new String();
	str_len = str.length;
	for(var i = 0;i<str_len;i++){
		a = str.charAt(i);
		str_length++;
		if(escape(a).length > 4){
			//中文字符的长度经编码之后大于4  
	 		str_length++;  
	 	}  
		str_cut = str_cut.concat(a);
		if(str_length>=len){
			str_cut = str_cut.concat("...");
			return str_cut;
		}  
	}  
	//如果给定字符串小于指定长度，则返回源字符串；
	if(str_length<len){
		return  str;
	}
}
function openJob() {
	$.post("teachingJob.action",function(data){
		var newFlg = data.newFlg;
		if (newFlg == true) {
			var homeworkCount = data.homeworkCount;
			var auditTeachersCount = data.auditTeachersCount;
			var auditStudentCount = data.auditStudentCount;
			var resourceCount = data.resourceCount;
			var forumpostsCount = data.forumpostsCount;
			var courseQuestionCount = data.courseQuestionCount;
			var jobHtml = "";
			if (homeworkCount != 0) {
					jobHtml += "<span style='margin-left:50px;margin-bottom:20px;'>有" + homeworkCount + "个待批阅的作业；</span></br>";
			}
			if (auditTeachersCount != 0) {
					jobHtml += "<span style='margin-left:50px;margin-bottom:20px;'>有" + auditTeachersCount + "位需审核的教师；</span></br>";
			}
			if (auditStudentCount != 0) {
					jobHtml += "<span style='margin-left:50px;margin-bottom:20px;'>有" + auditStudentCount + "位需审核的学生；</span></br>";
			}
			if (resourceCount != 0) {
					jobHtml += "<span style='margin-left:50px;margin-bottom:20px;'>有" + resourceCount + "条需审核的资源；</span></br>";
			}
			if (forumpostsCount != 0) {
					jobHtml += "<span style='margin-left:50px;margin-bottom:20px;'>有" + forumpostsCount + "个待审核的帖子；</span></br>";
			}
			if (courseQuestionCount != 0) {
					jobHtml += "<span style='margin-left:50px;margin-bottom:20px;'>有" + courseQuestionCount + "个待审核的问题；</span>";
			}
// 					var jobNewStyle = document.getElementById("teachingJobNew");
// 					jobNewStyle.style.color = "#ff7f0a";
// 					jobNewStyle.style.fontWeight = "bold";
// 					$("#teachingJobNew").html("<a href='javascript:openJobWin();'>您有未完成的工作！</a>");
			$("#teacherJob").html(jobHtml);
			openJobWin();
		}
		else {
// 					var jobNewStyle = document.getElementById("teachingJobNew");
// 					jobNewStyle.style.color = "#000";
// 					jobNewStyle.style.fontWeight = "normal";
			alertShow("您没有未完成的工作。");
		}
	},
	"JSON");
}

function openJobWin() {
	openWin("#teacherJobWin");
}
function closeJobWin(){
	$(".winCover").remove();
	$("#teacherJobWin").hide();
	$("#imgCrop").html("");
}

	$(".winCover").remove();
	$("#czloginBox").hide();
	$("#imgCrop").html("");
}

function clickHelp(){
	var url = useHelp;							//转向网页的地址;
	var name = "使用帮助";						//网页名称，可为空;
	var iWidth = "800";							//弹出窗口的宽度;
	var iHeight = "900";						//弹出窗口的高度;
	//获得窗口的垂直位置
	var iTop = (window.screen.availHeight-30-iHeight)/2;
	//获得窗口的水平位置
	var iLeft = (window.screen.availWidth-10-iWidth)/2;
	window.open(url,name,'height='+iHeight+',,innerHeight='+iHeight+',width='+iWidth+',innerWidth='+iWidth+',top='+iTop+',left='+iLeft+',status=no,toolbar=no,menubar=no,location=no,resizable=no,scrollbars=yes,titlebar=no');
}

	window.location.href = "http://202/cas/logout?service=http://210.29.166.212:80//userExit.action";
}

		function close(){
			var noMenuStr = $("#noMenuHidden").val();
				if(noMenuStr == undefined || noMenuStr == ""){
					$.ajax({
					url:"changeRoleMenuSessionNull.action",
					type:"post",
					async:false,
					success:function(data){
					},
					error:function(e,m){
					}
				});
				return;
			}
			$.ajax({
				url:"changeRoleMenuSessionTrue.action",
				type:"post",
				async:false,
				success:function(data){
				},
				error:function(e,m){
				}
			});
		}
		window.onbeforeunload=close;
		if("" != ""){
			$("#switch-btn").css({"background-position":"-335px -39px"});
			$(".sub-con").css({"display":"none"});
			$(".main-con").css({"margin-left":"0"});
			$("#switch-btn").attr("id","switch-bt");
			$("#isSequence").val(false);
		}
		$(document).ready(function(){
// 			if("" != ""){
// 				$("#switch-btn").css({"background-position":"-335px -39px"});
// 			    $(".sub-con").css({"display":"none"});
// 			    $(".main-con").css({"margin-left":"0"});
// 			    $("#switch-btn").attr("id","switch-bt");
// 			    $("#isSequence").val(false);
// 			}
			
			$("#span1").hover(
				function(){
					$(".resource_left a.res_edit_new").css("background-position","-26px -223px");
				},
				function(){
					$(".resource_left a.res_edit_new").css("background-position","-270px -77px");
				}
			);
			$("#span2").hover(
				function(){
					$("#span2 a").css("background","url('http://210.29.166.212:80/images/menuSetOrange.png')  no-repeat");
				},
				function(){
					$("#span2 a").css("background","url('http://210.29.166.212:80/images/img_bg.jpg') no-repeat -271px -108px");
				}
			);
			
			//展开或折叠菜单 start
			$("#leftMenu .button").click(function(event){
				if($(this).parent().next().size()>0){
					var showOrHide=$(this).parent().next().css("display");
					if(showOrHide == "none"){
						$(this).parent().next().show();
						$(this).removeClass("ico_close");
						$(this).addClass("ico_open");
					}else if(showOrHide == "block"){
						$(this).parent().next().hide();
						$(this).removeClass("ico_open");
						$(this).addClass("ico_close");
					}
				}
				event.stopPropagation();
			})
			//展开或折叠菜单 end
			
			//点击菜单 start
			$("#leftMenu a").click(function(){
				var menuType = $(this).attr("menuType");
				var menuAction = $(this).attr("menuAction");
				var menuName=$(this).attr("menuName");
				var menuId = $(this).attr("menuId");
				
				if(menuAction.indexOf("?") != -1){
					menuAction+="&currentChoiceRoleMenuId="+menuId;
				}else{
					menuAction+="?currentChoiceRoleMenuId="+menuId;
				}
				
				$("#leftMenu").find(".curSelectedNode").removeClass("curSelectedNode");
				$(this).addClass("curSelectedNode");
				
				if(menuType == 1025002){
					var showOrHide=$(this).next().css("display");
					if(showOrHide == "none"){
						$(this).next().show();
						$(this).find(".button").removeClass("ico_close");
						$(this).find(".button").addClass("ico_open");
					}else if(showOrHide == "block"){
						$(this).next().hide();
						$(this).find(".button").removeClass("ico_open");
						$(this).find(".button").addClass("ico_close");
					}
					return;
				}
				if(menuType == 1025001){
					window.open(menuAction,'XX',' left=0,top=0,width='+ (screen.availWidth - 10) +',height='+ (screen.availHeight-50) +',scrollbars,resizable=yes,toolbar=no');
					return;
				}
				$.ajax({
					url:"saveEnterCourseMenu.action",
					type:"post",
					data:{"enterCourseNav":menuName,"roleMenuId":menuId,"enterCourseMenuHtml":$("#leftMenu").html()},
					dataType:"json",
					async:false,
					success:function(data){
						if(data.success){
							window.location.href="http://210.29.166.212:80/"+menuAction;
						}else{
							window.location.reload();
						}
					}
				});
			})
			//点击菜单 end
			
			$("#leftMenu a").each(function(){
				var menuType = $(this).attr("menuType");
				if(menuType == 1025002){
					$(this).css("cursor","default");
				}
			});
		});
		
		function toMenuEdit(){
			confirmShow(
					"<ul>"+
						"<li style='padding: 10px 5px;'>"+

						"<li style='padding: 10px 5px;text-align: left;'>"+
						"3.重新关联菜单会删除当前菜单原有学习记录"+
						"</li>"+
						"<li style='padding: 10px 5px;text-align: left;'>"+
						"4.修改菜单后请检查评价指标配置是否变动"+
						"</li>"+
					"</ul>",
					function() {
						window.location.href = "toMenuEdit.action";
					});
		}
